</div><div class="az-page-breadcrumbs"></div></div></div><div class="site-inner"><div class="content-sidebar-wrap"><p style="padding-top: 10px">The Arizona Revised Statutes have been updated to include the revised sections from the 54th Legislature, 2nd  Regular Session.  Please note that the next update of this compilation will not take place until after the conclusion of the 55th Legislature, 1st Regular Session, which convenes in January 2021.</p><h6><u>DISCLAIMER</u></h6><p>This online version of the Arizona Revised Statutes is primarily maintained for legislative drafting purposes and reflects the version of law that is effective on January 1st of the year following the most recent legislative session.  The official version of the Arizona Revised Statutes is published by Thomson Reuters.</p><div><h1 class="topTitle">Title 36 - Public Health and Safety</h1><div class="five-sixths first"><div
